#HISTORY The output FITS files contain a 3-D array of data consisting of setsof  
#HISTORY  triplet arrays of data for each aperture and each order, whereeach tr  
#HISTORY iplet is composed of an array for the wavelength, an array forthe flux  
#HISTORY , and an array for the error. The triplets for each apertureare stacke  
#HISTORY d behind one another, followed by the triplets for the nextorder, etc.  
#HISTORY  If no orders have been skipped or deslected in theextraction process,  
#HISTORY  the contents of aperture Y in order X can befound as follows:lambda =  
#HISTORY  array[*,0,( X - (smallest ordernumber))*naps + (Y-1)], flux   = array  
#HISTORY [*,1,( X - (smallest ordernumber))*naps + (Y-1)], error  = array[*,2,(  
#HISTORY  X - (smallest ordernumber))*naps + (Y-1)]  For example, for an SXD fi  
#HISTORY le with twoapertures, the wavelength array for aperture 1 in order 3 i  
#HISTORY s locatedin array [*,0,0], the flux is in array [*,1,0] and the error   
#HISTORY is inarray [*,2,0]. For aperture 2, the wavelength is in array [*,0,1]  
#HISTORY ,the flux is in array [*,1,1] and the error is in array [*,2,1]. Foror  
#HISTORY der 4, the flux for aperture 1 is in array [*,1,2], while the fluxfor   
#HISTORY aperture 2 is in array [*,1,3]. For order 5, the fluxes for thetwo ape  
#HISTORY rtures are in arrays [*,1,4] and [*,1,5], etc.  The spectrahave been c  
#HISTORY orrected for non-linearity.
